The Special District Telephone Price Increase is Near - Citywide Users are Resolutely Fighting - The Telephone Committee Sends Letters Requesting Separate Meetings - Vowing to Persist Until a Satisfactory Resolution is Achieved 125

The Dagong News Agency reports: The Special District Telephone Issue Committee of this city, considering that the implementation period for the Special District telephone price increase is approaching, has sent letters to both Chinese and foreign taxpayer associations, requesting that a taxpayer meeting be convened to discuss fundamental cancellation methods. However, no news has been received as of yet. In preparation for the final struggle, the committee has scheduled an executive committee meeting for the 12th of this month to discuss countermeasures. In addition, the committee has sent a letter to the Citizens' Federation, requesting that it instruct its district branches to convene joint meetings of telephone users separately, to adopt the same steps to facilitate progress. The details are recorded below:

Willing to Sacrifice if a Resolution is Not Achieved

The Special District Telephone Issue Committee sent a letter to the First Special District and Second Special District Citizens' Federations the other day, stating: Respectfully, the Shanghai Telephone Company is effectively increasing prices in disguise, and the collection of fees is imminent. However, as it concerns the economic interests of citizens and affects the entire business community, all citizens are rising up in opposition. It is understood that telephones are a public utility intended to facilitate society. Therefore, the remuneration obtained from business operations cannot be equated with profit-generating commerce. The company uses the agreement with the Municipal Council to charge an official interest rate of one percent as an excuse to arbitrarily increase prices, disregarding the interests of the public, which is a grave mistake. Shanghai's commerce, since January 28th, has declined to its lowest point. The expensive houses in the concessions of the past are now unwanted. Although the number of telephone users has not decreased, it is due to business relationships and they dare not dismantle them easily. The company is acting monopolistically and selfishly, oppressing the citizens, which is not permissible in terms of reason and emotion. In addition to scheduling an executive committee meeting to discuss the final countermeasures, this committee is writing to your association to inform all citizens that, until a satisfactory resolution is achieved, they are willing to sacrifice everything and persist to achieve the final goal. Furthermore, we request that you promptly notify the district branches to convene users throughout the district to discuss resistance measures, in order to take the same steps. Time is of the essence. We hope you will investigate and act accordingly. (Dagong News Agency)

Sending Letters to Various Organizations to Solicit Opinions

The Special District Telephone Issue Committee sent letters to various trade associations in this city yesterday, stating: Respectfully, the Shanghai Telephone Company, in order to satisfy its desire for an annual interest rate of one percent, has formulated new fee regulations that will be implemented starting March 1st. In this autumn of economic downturn and industrial and commercial stagnation, how can we bear further burdens? All of our trade organizations should consider the situation from the perspective of their members and users, and work together to resist. Your association is a group of merchants in a certain industry and should actively seek benefits for all members to gradually reduce the economic panic so that recovery can be hoped for and restoration can be expected. Moreover, telephones are a tool to improve commercial communication, and once restricted by per-call fees, they will be an invisible constraint, and the intangible losses to the industry will be incalculable. This committee witnesses this with heartache and cannot remain silent. Therefore, we are sending this letter to solicit your opinions, so that we can gather wisdom and unite to make the most resolute expression and forceful resistance. (Guowen News Agency)

Telephone Committee Discussing Countermeasures Again

The Special District Telephone Issue Committee, considering that the telephone price increase is approaching, has scheduled the third board of directors meeting for 3:00 PM on the 12th of this month at the City Merchant Association in Tianhougong Bridge to prepare countermeasures, and has invited all advisory committee members to attend to discuss the matter together. However, the committee's responsibilities are heavy and difficult to handle. In addition to sending letters to various legal entities requesting that they uphold justice, the committee will convene a joint meeting of representatives from various organizations to solicit public opinion, as the committee is formed by various organizations, and its advocacy must comply with the public opinion of those organizations. District Branches Preparing for Resistance

The forty-one district branches of the First Special District Citizens' Federation, in order to oppose the telephone price increase issue, jointly sent a letter to the Chinese Taxpayers Association the other day, requesting that a taxpayer meeting be convened to discuss the overall solution. Jiangsu Province Actively Improving Sericulture 130

Ordering High-Quality Silkworm Eggs for Distribution to Farmers for Breeding - Ordering 850,000 Mulberry Saplings and Instructing Various Counties to Plant Them

The Shenshi News Agency reports that the Jiangsu Provincial Sericulture Improvement Management Committee believes that farmers have been following outdated practices in silkworm rearing for years, resulting in low cocoon prices and economic hardship for farmers. Therefore, it has established a sericulture experiment station and sent personnel to Japan to order spring silkworm eggs for sale to farmers. It has borrowed 160,000 yuan from the Jiangsu Bank and other sources for distribution to farmers, enabling them to obtain high-quality eggs and improve rearing methods. This is now actively underway. The committee believes that most of the mulberry trees planted by farmers in various places were planted more than a decade ago, resulting in dry and old mulberry leaves, which has an impact on the future of silkworm rearing. The reason for this is the collapse of the rural economy and the drastic drop in cocoon prices, leaving farmers unable to afford to purchase mulberry saplings and plant new mulberry trees. If improvements are not sought, the sericulture industry will be completely bankrupt. Therefore, it has purchased 800,000 high-quality mulberry saplings from Zhejiang Province and received 50,000 improved mulberry saplings from the National Economic Commission for distribution to farmers in various counties for planting. The committee will also send personnel to guide planting methods, ensuring improvement. Once successful results are achieved, it plans to completely replant all old mulberry trees, gradually bringing the sericulture industry in our country onto a bright path.

Last Year's Import of Shark Fins and Sea Cucumbers Reached Over Two Million Yuan 132

Japanese Goods Accounted for the Majority

The Riri News Agency reports that shark fins and sea cucumbers are valuable foods, and our country imports several million yuan worth each year. According to the International Trade Bureau, the total import of shark fins and sea cucumbers nationwide last year reached over 2.5 million yuan, with Japanese goods accounting for the most. The import volume of shark fins was 7.334 metric tons from Aden, 18.529 metric tons from India, 50.080 metric tons from Hong Kong, 419.028 metric tons from Japan, 8.893 metric tons from Siam, 69.177 metric tons from Singapore, and 41.236 metric tons from other countries. Excluding the re-export of 1.393 metric tons to foreign countries, the total export was 612.884 metric tons, valued at 287,426 customs gold units, equivalent to 531,935 national currency units. The import volume of sea cucumbers was 40.208 metric tons from Aden, 44.179 metric tons from Australia, 107.498 metric tons from Egypt, 234.372 metric tons from Hong Kong, 550.873 metric tons from Japan, 42.160 metric tons from Siam, 216.849 metric tons from the Dutch East Indies, 44.720 metric tons from the Philippines, 541.604 metric tons from Singapore, and 57.320 metric tons from other countries. Excluding the re-export of 231 metric tons to foreign countries, the total export was 1,879,552 metric tons, valued at 1,075,874 customs gold units, equivalent to 2,008,089 national currency units. The total import of shark fins amounted to 2,540,024 yuan.

Telegram from Mr. Pu Li, Owner of the Tongshun Ship - Regarding Grounding at Mofu Cape 133

Ship Hit a Sharp Rock - Forward Hold Flooded Five Feet - Please Send a Tugboat with a Water Pump Immediately - The Datongxing Shipping Company's Tongshun ship ran aground at Mofu Cape on February 5th while sailing from Fuzhou to Hongji to load coal. The ship owner, Pu Li, telegraphed the details of the incident and requested assistance. The United Insurance Association is discussing rescue measures. The details are as follows:

Ship Owner's Telegram - Details of the Grounding

The Tongshun ship, with a gross tonnage of 2,346 tons, departed from Fuzhou on February 5th after unloading cargo and sailed empty to Hongji to load coal for Shanghai. On February 8th at 9:00 AM, while sailing near Hainan Island at Mofa Point (Mofu Cape), it mistakenly ran aground. The bottom of the forward hold was damaged by a sharp rock, and seawater entered. The ship owner, Pu Li, immediately sent a wireless telegram for assistance. The Datongxing Shanghai Company on Sijing Road, Shanghai, received the report and Manager Zhou Zian discussed rescue measures with the China Ship Insurance Association, which underwrote the Ping'an Insurance.

Company Meeting - Planning Rescue

The Shanghai company received a subsequent telegram in English from Tongshun ship owner Pu Li at 9:00 AM yesterday morning, stating: "Ship hit a sharp rock, forward hold flooded five feet, ship's bow facing northeast, please send a tugboat immediately with a water pump to rescue." Manager Zhou has discussed with the Insurance Association and decided to telegraph Hainan Island to send a ship with a water pump to provide assistance.

All Crew Members Still on Board

The Tongshun ship has a total of 52 crew members, except for the ship owner who is Norwegian, all others are Chinese. Although the ship has run aground and the forward hold is flooded, all crew members are still on board as no ship has been sent for rescue. If the weather does not change significantly, it is expected that the crew members will be safe. Currently, the families of the crew members hope that the company will send a ship as soon as possible to rescue them, to avoid any danger to the lives of the crew members.

The Special Second Court Tried the Case of Guo Yuzhou's False Accusation 137

Closing Arguments Concluded - Sentencing on the 14th

Guo Yuzhou, a Cantonese businessman from Chaozhou who was twice kidnapped for ransom, is 57 years old this year and resides at No. 1 Yuyang Lane, Berville Road, in the French Concession, which is his own property. He previously opened the Xiafei Apartment at the entrance of Yuyang Lane and hired Zhong Xin, a local, as manager. Last winter, Guo discovered that Zhong had embezzled 500 yuan and reported Zhong to the French police station for embezzlement. The police department filed a public prosecution with the Second Special District Court. After the trial, the defendant Zhong Xin was found not guilty. The police department, dissatisfied with the verdict, appealed to the Third High Court. After deliberation, the collegial panel dismissed the appeal. During the Third High Court's trial, the complainant Guo Yuzhou repeatedly failed to appear in court. The prosecutor considered that the original complainant Guo Yuzhou was indeed suspected of making a false accusation and transferred the case to the Special Second Court Procuratorate for investigation and prosecution to deter frivolous lawsuits. After the prosecutor Wang Ren of the Special Second Court summoned the defendant Guo Yuzhou to court for investigation, he determined that Guo's false accusation was true and ordered Guo to pay 300 yuan in cash bail to be released pending further investigation. He then filed a public prosecution with the criminal court of the same level for the crime of false accusation under Article 169, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law. The trial was held the other day in the Second Criminal Court by Judge Xiong Hui Ping together with Prosecutor Wang. First, the prosecutor stated the intent of the prosecution. The defendant Guo Yuzhou appeared with his defense lawyer. Guo stated that Zhong Xin had been working as a merchant for seven or eight years, and he had always trusted him. On August 29th of last year, he gave him money to purchase goods. Unexpectedly, on September 3rd, Zhong suddenly announced his separation from the merchant, and the accounts were not handed over. After checking, he discovered that Zhong had embezzled more than 500 yuan, so he reported it to the police station and did not make a false accusation. His lawyer then made a defense. The court declared the closing arguments concluded and scheduled the sentencing for the 14th. The defendant was ordered to remain on the original bail.

Impersonating French Police Officers for Extortion 138

Three Defendants Arrested Successively - Li Xushi Recounts the Incident

Li Xushi, a 39-year-old woman from Yangzhou living at No. 4 Rongshen Lane, Menggu Road, Zhabei, previously reported to the French police station that her husband, Li Yuanshou, was arrested and sent to the Nanshi District Court on May 13th of last year for a murder case. On June 7th, two fellow villagers, Zhang Guangxi (27 years old, employee of the Samsung Barber Shop at No. 491 Kangti Road) and Luo Laosan (39 years old, employee of the Dong'an Barber Shop at No. 656 Xipushi Road), together with Liu Changgui, a fellow villager living at No. 36 Ning'an Lane, Haining Road, came to her house. Zhang and Luo claimed that Liu was a bailiff of the court and held a court warrant to arrest her for questioning. She was shocked and pleaded with them. Zhang and Luo then claimed that they could settle the case if she paid 420 yuan. She agreed and scraped together 200 yuan and wrote an IOU for 220 yuan. On July 27th, she borrowed 100 yuan from Wang Xiaolaizi at the South Wharf and gave it to Zhang and Luo. On August 3rd, she borrowed another 120 yuan from Zhou Wenliang on Sanma Road and gave it to Zhang, Luo, and Liu. However, they did not return the IOU after receiving the money. Recently, she went to the Nanshi District Court to find Liu Changgui and ask for the IOU back. People in the court replied that there was no one named Liu Changgui in the court serving as a bailiff. She then realized that Zhang, Luo, and Liu had colluded to defraud her of money and requested their arrest for investigation. The detective approved her request and sent investigators to arrest the two defendants Zhang and Luo and escort them to the Special Second Court for detention. Liu fled upon hearing the news. The court issued a warrant for his arrest. Recently, investigator Zhou Qingfang arrested Liu and escorted him to the court, where he was joined to the case. The case was continued in the Eighth Criminal Court the other day by Judge Sun Pengxian of the Special Third Court. The complainant Li Xushi recounted the defendants' fraud. The three defendants Zhang, Luo, and Liu confessed that they had committed the fraud. They also claimed that the plaintiff lived by working as a domestic helper. How could she have such a large sum of money to be defrauded? They requested an investigation. The court verified the statements and, as the case required further detailed investigation, ordered that they be detained pending investigation and rescheduled the hearing. The defendants were returned to custody.

All Related Parties Were Prosecuted

Shen Er Nian, a woman from Jiaxing who is now 18 years old, was sold to Xu Abao, a woman from Suzhou who operated a brothel at No. 17 Yingchun Lane, Hubei Road, for 250 yuan in August of last year at the Shenjiang Hotel on Hankou Road to work as a prostitute. From then on, Shen fell into a fiery pit, suffering endless trampling and misery. Sometimes, because she could not receive patrons, she was whipped by Xu, no different from a living hell. Recently, Shen, unable to bear the suffering, took advantage of Xu's negligence and secretly escaped the other day, seeking relief at the Old City Gate police station. Western detective Fang Tai'er and Chinese detective Chen Shanji went and first arrested Xu Abao. Then, they went to No. 23 Hongfu Lane, Xinzha Road, and arrested the original introducer, Ni Guicai from Jiangbei, and brought them back to the police station. Yesterday, they were escorted to the First Criminal Court of the Special First Court. Police attorney Wang Yaotang stated the details and filed a prosecution under Article 241 of the Criminal Law. Then, Shen Er Nian submitted a petition describing her being sold and abused. Judge Qian Hongye questioned the two defendants and ordered them to be detained, pending rescheduling of the hearing.

Major Drug Trafficking Suspect Qin Cainan Ordered to Find Bail 141

Former Guarantor Requests Withdrawal

Qin Cainan, a Wuxi native involved in an international drug trafficking case, was arrested by the French police in the summer of the 22nd year [of the Republic, i.e., 1933] and brought before the Special District Court, which sentenced him to imprisonment and a fine. During the appeal period, he was released on bail with a 5,000 yuan cash deposit and a 10,000 yuan joint guarantee from three businesses. After being released on bail, Qin appealed the verdict to the Higher Third Branch Court, but the appeal was rejected. His father then appealed to the Supreme Court, which overturned the original verdict and sent the case back to the Higher Third Branch Court for retrial. As previously reported, the Higher Third Branch Court has issued documents to various relevant government offices to assist in the investigation. However, during the appeal period, two of the original three guarantor businesses closed due to the poor economy. The remaining guarantor, Pan Chicheng, the owner of a cosmetics factory, requested to withdraw his guarantee due to the large sum involved. Qin claimed illness and did not appear in court. As a result, Hong Xiangtao, the owner of Yushun Rice Store on Rue Garafilo, and a coal store jointly guaranteed 5,000 yuan and Qin paid a 5,000 yuan cash deposit. Pan Chicheng, the original guarantor who withdrew, alleged that Qin's family had made extortion attempts, leading to a lawsuit in the Special District Court's criminal division for defamation. Recently, the new guarantors, Hong Xiangtao and others, heard rumors that Qin was liquidating his assets and leaving Shanghai. They filed a petition with the Higher Third Branch Court requesting to withdraw their guarantee. The court ordered Qin to find new guarantors within a specified period. Qin only managed to deposit 1,000 yuan, and could not find any new guarantors. The Higher Third Branch Court summoned Hong Xiangtao for questioning and the next day summoned Qin for questioning. Qin arrived at the court accompanied by his concubine and defense lawyer. After questioning by Judge Sun, Qin was ordered to quickly find guarantors within three days, or else the 4,000 yuan deposit would be confiscated. Qin complied and left.

Tragedy in a Hotel 143

Borrowed Clothes Pawned and Not Redeemed for a Long Time: Fang Baoqing Stabbed by a Friend

Fang Baoqing, a local Shanghainese, 34 years old, residing at 282 Youyi Lane, Balizhao Road, French Concession, has no occupation. Recently, since it was the New Year, he had been going to his friend's room in the Central Hotel on Wuma Road every day to hang out. Another friend, Mr. Jia, had recently pawned Fang's overcoat for eight yuan due to financial difficulties, promising to return it by a certain date. However, the deadline had long passed, and Mr. Jia had not redeemed it. Yesterday afternoon around 6:30 PM, Fang and Mr. Jia met again at the entrance of the staircase on the second floor of the Central Hotel. Fang immediately demanded repayment, and the two got into an argument. Unexpectedly, in a fit of anger, Mr. Jia suddenly rushed to the barber shop on the second floor, grabbed a pair of scissors, ran out, and without asking any questions, stabbed Fang in the right waist. Fang was unable to dodge in time and was stabbed, falling to the ground in pain. The assailant fled in the chaos. By the time the hotel staff arrived, the assailant had already escaped. They immediately reported to the police station. The head detective immediately led Chinese and foreign detectives to the scene and sent Fang to Renji Hospital for treatment. They also took a barber to the police station for investigation. Afterwards, they captured a suspect and took him to the hospital for Fang to identify. According to Fang, although this person was not the actual assailant, he was definitely an accomplice. Fang's injuries are said to be very serious.

Shanghai Telephone Company Announces: Economic "Pay Per Call" 146

According to the Shanghai Telephone Company, after the Public Concession and French Concession municipal councils approved the implementation of the new pay-per-call telephone rates on March 1, users generally want to understand the economic impact. On the surface, the new rates seem like a general price increase, but this is not the case. The telephone company has conducted detailed surveys of monthly call volumes for residential and business users over the past two years to serve as a standard for the new rates. Based on the survey results, nearly half of the residential and business users will reduce their telephone expenses due to the new rates. Furthermore, the pay-per-call method is not a new experiment. Since 1925, ten years ago, hotels, clubs, tea houses, and other institutions that serve many citizens have been charged per call. The new rates will also benefit these users, because the basic rate has been reduced, and the overage rate has been cut in half to three cents per call, whereas it was previously six cents.

Li Dijun Arrives in Shanghai to Discuss Ministry of Foreign Affairs Revising Diplomatic Dictionary, and Compiling Treaties Signed with Various Countries 149

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, Li Dijun, director of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Information Department, arrived in Shanghai by express train from Beijing at around 7 AM the day before yesterday for official business. He stayed at the New Asia Hotel on Tiantong Road. After completing his business, he returned to Beijing on the 11 PM express train last night. Former Director of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Information Department, Zhang Sixu, hosted a banquet for Li Dijun the night before last, with Mayor Wu Tiecheng of this city and others in attendance, and invited reporters from various foreign newspapers in Shanghai to meet Mr. Li. Yesterday morning, Li Dijun told a Xin Sheng News Agency reporter that the Ministry of Foreign Affairs currently has two important tasks: one is to revise the diplomatic dictionary, and the other is to compile all of the treaties that our country has signed with various countries over the years. The former task has a special committee for revising the diplomatic dictionary, which will handle comparisons in Chinese, English, and French, making it relatively easy. The latter task is more troublesome because it must be compiled into separate volumes. Except for the Sino-American and Sino-Japanese treaties, which have already been compiled and only need to be supplemented, the others, such as the Sino-British, Sino-French, and Sino-Belgian treaties, must be traced back to their origins and compiled. It will inevitably take a long time to complete.

New Price List Implemented by Silk and Satin Dyeing Industry, Monthly Billing 154

The Shanghai Silk and Satin Dyeing Industry Association recently raised raw material prices and old dyeing prices which are calculated per piece cannot offset the material prices, resulting in large losses. Moreover, the length of silk pieces varies daily and the unlimited expansion should be abolished to save the industry. At the last general meeting, it was resolved that from this year, the dyeing prices for all silk pieces will be calculated in municipal meters, and a new price list will be established based on municipal meter calculations. During the revision of dyeing prices, the current socio-economic conditions were carefully considered, the policy of price control and equalization was implemented, and the corrupt habit of price competition among the same industry in the future was eliminated. At the same time, dyeing was carefully improved, and the interests of both the silk and dyeing industries were promoted. Recently, various industries have been advertising "monthly billing" to facilitate the flow of finance and materials. The silk industry is handling acceptance bills of exchange to cope with the recession, opening a source of motivation. The dyeing industry and the silk industry are closely related, and in this economic trend, it was decided to adopt monthly billing to promote cooperation. This suggestion has been voted on, a consent form has been prepared, and the price list has been printed. A general meeting will be convened tomorrow to distribute the forms, which will be forwarded to various silk shops for approval. If any silk shop disregards these regulations and hesitates to postpone the discussion, the association will take emergency measures and implement a dyeing suspension policy.

逕啟者、茲據敝當事人鍾長源等來所聲稱、閱本月九日申報登有軍帽業勞包糾紛新聞一則、內載各節、悉與事實不符、查鄙人等前因遵守局訂勞包契的、迭經函催勞方來廠工作、詛彼方百端留難、極盡要挾能事、包方因交貨期迫、為維持信用計、免損害賠償責任計、迫不得已、依的取正當之方法、招工裁製、藉完承攬人義務、奈勞方不惜觸犯刑章、共同以强暴脅迫行為、率眾直闖廠中、肆意倒亂、危詞恐嚇、一時秩序紛亂、旋法捕房聞訊、派警趕至、扭拘主犯、並扣留供犯罪之用之什具、眾犯乘機竄散、報載云云、似失實情、委請代表、致函史正、免淆聽聞、等情前米、據此、相應函請貴報館迅賜更正、實級公誼、此致

To the Editor,

We are writing on behalf of our clients, Zhong Changyuan, et al., who have stated that the news item regarding a labor dispute in the military cap industry published in the Shen Bao on the 9th of this month contains details that are inconsistent with the facts. Our clients have been adhering to the labor contract established by the bureau and have repeatedly sent letters urging the labor side to return to work. However, the labor side has created numerous obstacles and engaged in excessive extortion. Due to the urgency of the delivery deadline, and in order to maintain credibility and avoid liability for damages, the contractors were compelled to employ legitimate methods to recruit workers and complete production, thereby fulfilling their contractual obligations. However, the labor side, disregarding criminal laws, collectively engaged in violent and coercive behavior, leading a crowd to storm the factory, causing intentional disruption and issuing threatening language, resulting in temporary chaos. Upon receiving the news, the French police dispatched officers to arrest the principal offenders and seize the instruments used for the crime. The other offenders took the opportunity to flee. The report in the newspaper appears to be inaccurate. We have been entrusted to write to clarify the situation to prevent confusion. We respectfully request your newspaper to promptly issue a correction. Sincerely,

To: Shen Bao Newspaper Office,

Lawyer Wang Xintang, February 9th,

主筆先生台鑒、閱七日貴報有「無名男子輾死一節、與事實不符、特此函懇更正、該男子係本行工人、工作已有十二年之久、姓何、名大徵、平日行為謹慎、此决被十路公共汽車輾斃、係該路公共汽車駛行太速之故、然是非自有公論、不願多贅、但請更正如上、且該工人上有老母、下有妻女、境况十分悽慘云、此請撰安、

To the Esteemed Editor,

Having read your newspaper's report on the 7th regarding the "unidentified man run over and killed," we find it inconsistent with the facts. We are writing to request a correction. The deceased man was a worker at our firm, having worked here for twelve years. His surname was He, and his given name was Dazheng. He was usually very careful. He was killed by the Number 10 bus, which was traveling too fast. Right and wrong are clear to all, so we will not elaborate further. Please make the correction as stated above. Furthermore, the worker leaves behind an elderly mother, a wife, and daughters, and their situation is extremely dire. We wish you peace.

Lao Jinlong Foreign Firm,

The defending Scott Cup champion Donghua team played against Xishang in the Scott Cup semi-finals at the Shenyuan Stadium. The spring snow had just melted, making the field extremely muddy and slippery. The players from both teams stumbled and fell repeatedly, each becoming a clay Buddha. After the opening, Xishang was exceptionally agile, trading blows and achieving a tie. Donghua, relying on Sun's "Iron Leg" for three goals, took a 3-2 lead. In the second half, Donghua's players were incredibly fierce, scoring three more goals in a row. Xishang, however, collapsed and achieved nothing, ultimately being eliminated by Donghua with a score of 2-6. Yesterday, the stands at Shenyuan were not as crowded as the previous week's semi-final match between Spain and Portugal. The four stands had mostly empty seats, with only about a thousand spectators. More than half of Xishang's players in yesterday's match were veterans, supplemented by newcomers, making the game still worth watching. The lineups for the two teams are as follows:

The two teams repeatedly advanced and retreated. At six minutes, Jia Youliang got the ball and crossed it. Li Yichen flicked it slightly, and Sun Jinshun added a shot, opening the scoring. From the center line, Xishang launched a fierce attack, creating chaos in front of Donghua's goal. Li Ning forced a corner kick. Aigraifu kicked it perfectly, and Li Ning headed it out of danger again. In an instant, there was another chaotic situation in front of Donghua's goal. Xishang's central defender, Jack, headed the ball, which bounced back off the left post. Huo Wei headed it again, and Changjiao Lu hurriedly saved it, barely touching the edge. The ball spun around the goal line. The clock showed nine minutes at one to one.

西聯足球甲組賽　優游力失挫西捕　三比一

West League First Division Soccer Match: You You Defeats Xi Bu Three to One

優游合作佳妙小黑炭尤見神勇　西捕長力不濟僅海爾射中一球

You You's Cooperation Was Excellent, and Little Black Coal Was Especially Courageous; Xi Bu Lacked Stamina, with Only Hair Scoring a Goal

西聯會甲組足球聯賽、優游對西捕、昨日下午三時在膠州路膠州公園交鋒、優游出題以來、每戰皆捷、對於甲組錦標、虎視眈眈、西捕亦係滬上強隊之一、在本屆史高托盃中、曾以三對　淘汰優游、昨日仇人重逢、雙方均出全力相爭、故慕名前往作壁上觀者、約三四千人、實開公園開賽足球以來、未有之紀錄、上半時優游全軍合作、由小黑炭在終了前約三分鐘攻入一球、以一對〇佔優、下半時、西捕抱破斧沈舟决心、反攻甚烈、惜長力不濟、及遭優游諸將趁虛而入、又以二對一再勝、總結果三對一優游凱旋、雙方陣容如下、

In the West League First Division soccer league, You You faced Xi Bu at Jiaozhou Park on Jiaozhou Road at 3:00 PM yesterday. Since its debut, You You has won every match and is eyeing the First Division championship. Xi Bu is also one of Shanghai's strong teams and eliminated You You in this year's Scott Cup with a score of 3-0. Yesterday, the rivals met again, and both sides fought with all their might. Therefore, about three to four thousand people came to watch, setting a record for the most spectators since the park started hosting soccer matches. In the first half, You You cooperated well, and Little Black Coal scored a goal about three minutes before the end, taking a 1-0 lead. In the second half, Xi Bu was determined to win and launched a fierce counterattack. Unfortunately, they lacked stamina and were taken advantage of by You You's players, who won again by a score of 2-1. The final result was 3-1, and You You triumphed. The lineups for both sides are as follows:

西捕隊姗姗來遲

The Xi Bu Team Arrived Late

優游隊首先上場、試練脚頭、比賽時間已屆、仍未見西捕隊降臨、迨三時一刻、始姗姗遲來、裁判員陳吉祥銀角聲起、兩隊佈陣而戰、優游隊先取攻勢、鍾育祥脚下撥動阿斗、輸運前敵、小黑炭旁敲側擊、連闖三關、番將克勞福眼看形勢不佳、斜裏竄出、攔住去路、鐘育祥崛起中原、繞道逼入西捕腹地、阿崙躍起揮出、鐘被吉勃生搿位踣地、致未命中、敵將漢萊中路率兵來犯、盤運至相當地域、舉脚攻門、張榮才手脚玲快、振臂盤出、安渡難關、透納東山再起、兵臨優游陣前、海爾強弩冷放、張榮才躍起一托、擊中自己門柱、幸未吿失守、亦云險哉、

The You You team was the first to take the field, practicing their kicks. The game time had arrived, but the Xi Bu team had not yet appeared. It was not until 3:15 PM that they arrived late. The referee Chen Jixiang blew the whistle, and the two teams lined up to fight. The You You team took the offensive first, with Zhong Yuxiang dribbling the ball and passing it to the front line. Little Black Coal attacked from the side, breaking through three barriers in a row. Seeing that the situation was not good, the foreign general Crawford darted out diagonally to block the way. Zhong Yuxiang rose from the Central Plains, detouring and forcing his way into the heart of Xi Bu's territory. Alun jumped up and swung, but Zhong was tripped by Jibson, causing him to miss. The enemy general Hanlai led his troops to attack from the middle, dribbling to a suitable area and kicking the ball at the goal. Zhang Rongcai was quick with his hands and feet, waving his arms and batting the ball out, safely weathering the storm. Turner made a comeback, and his troops approached the front of You You's position. Hair fired a cold arrow, and Zhang Rongcai jumped up to block it, hitting his own goalpost. Fortunately, they did not lose the goal, which was also a dangerous situation.

小黑炭首開紀錄

Little Black Coal Opens the Scoring

劉矮子始讚、邊陲揭竿起義、與許竟成搭擋、三傳五遞、已入西捕深地、許竟成射來、過高越門飛過、此時西捕聲勢大盛、前鋒諸將勢如風捲殘葉般殺奔優游陣地、何奈江陳兩將、保衛如銅牆鐵欄、致三過茅蘆而不入、威利因賣力過甚、受傷出塲、優游隊乘隙反攻、鐘勇森邊陲入寇、銳不可當、風陷西捕防地、立傳中央、王南珍趕之不及、良機坐失、威利乃負傷重行上塲、此後勢常在西捕境內徘徊、優游諸將活躍異常、圍攻敵門、險象環生、惜兩度越位、無功而返、鐘勇森再接再厲、運兵邊域、轉傳敵軍深地、小黑炭迎之以頭、頂上開花、紀錄首開、未三分鐘時間吿終、優游以二對〇佔先、

Liu Aizi began to praise, and the border uprisings rose up, partnering with Xu Jingcheng. After three passes and five deliveries, they had entered deep into Xi Bu's territory. Xu Jingcheng shot, but it flew too high and over the goal. At this time, Xi Bu's momentum was strong, and the forward generals rushed to the You You camp like a whirlwind sweeping away fallen leaves. However, the two generals Jiang and Chen defended like copper walls and iron fences, preventing them from entering. Willie was injured and left the field due to excessive effort. The You You team took the opportunity to counterattack, and Zhong Yongshen invaded from the border, unstoppable, falling into Xi Bu's defense and establishing a central position. Wang Nanzhen failed to catch up, and the good opportunity was lost. Willie returned to the field with injuries. After this, the momentum often lingered in Xi Bu's territory. You You's generals were extremely active, besieging the enemy's goal, creating dangerous situations, but unfortunately, they were offside twice and returned without success. Zhong Yongshen continued to work hard, transporting troops to the border and transferring them to the enemy's deep territory. Little Black Coal greeted them with his head, opening the scoring. Before three minutes had passed, the time was up, and You You led 2-0.

海爾力射成和局

Hair's Powerful Shot Results in a Tie

檸檬過後、易地再戰、西捕抱破斧沈舟决心、謀雪前恥、故全軍奮發、戰來有聲有色、尤以軋許搶球欄刦、別具功夫、不塊為大將之才、奈前鋒諸將所任職位、都未能發展、致失却聯絡、遂至一蹶不振、廻顧優游諸將聲勢凌人、鐘育祥統領三軍、浩浩蕩蕩、侵略西捕內地、兩捕境內乃敵騎滿佈、橫遭蹂躪、鐘勇森見機、由邊疆帶球繞道而進、匹馬單鎗、不計利害、深入虎穴、阿崙出阻擋互撞、兩人同時倒地、球由門前越過、向左滾去、王南珍不忙不慌、趕上命中、惜越位作廢、西捕難期旣渡、傑克邊境謀反、大刀闊斧、連闖三關、乃施調虎離山計、瞞過江善敬、立傳中軍、張榮才不該衝出搶球、海爾枕戈以待、從容踢入網角、構成和局、

After the intermission, the two teams changed sides and fought again. Xi Bu was determined to avenge their previous defeat, so the entire army was invigorated and fought vigorously. In particular, Zhaxu was skilled in stealing the ball, and was a talented general. However, the positions held by the forward generals were not able to develop, resulting in a loss of contact, and they were unable to recover. Looking back, You You's generals were aggressive, and Zhong Yuxiang commanded the three armies,浩浩蕩蕩, invading Xi Bu's inland. The two captured areas were filled with enemy cavalry and were ravaged. Seeing the opportunity, Zhong Yongshen took the ball from the border and detoured, advancing with one horse and one gun, regardless of the consequences, deep into the enemy's lair. Alun came out to block and collided, and the two fell to the ground at the same time. The ball crossed the goal from the front and rolled to the left. Wang Nanzhen was not in a hurry, caught up, and hit the goal, but unfortunately, it was offside and invalid. It was difficult for Xi Bu to cross over. Jack conspired against the border, advancing with great strides, breaking through three barriers in a row, and implementing a plan to lure the tiger away from the mountain, deceiving Jiang Shan Jing, and establishing a central army. Zhang Rongcai should not have rushed out to grab the ball. Hair waited with his spear and calmly kicked the ball into the corner of the net, creating a tie.

三比一優游獲勝

You You Wins 3-1

造成平手後、不啻是雙方緊急關頭、但西捕至此已戰得人困馬疲、不若先前之勇猛、然精神始終一貫、全軍仍努力奔跑、殊堪欽佩、鐘勇森截獲後方來球、帶球直闖、鐘育祥狼狽為奸、左右進逼、在西捕前據作一團、列始讚從人叢中穿出、挑動毛腿、敵鬥再破、陳鎭和接草運糧、鐘勇森捲土重來、一路勢破竹、連破敵軍駐兵、在邊綫十五碼叩門、清脆可觀、又吿中的、兩球之人、前後僅三分鐘、此後西捕雖作困獸之鬥、極力掙扎、奈時不我待、未幾、銀角長鳴、雙方鳴金息戈、結果優游三對一奪得勝利而歸、

After creating a tie, it was undoubtedly a critical moment for both sides, but Xi Bu had fought to the point of exhaustion and was no longer as brave as before. However, their spirit remained consistent, and the entire army continued to run hard, which was admirable. Zhong Yongshen intercepted the ball coming from the rear and dribbled straight in. Zhong Yuxiang acted as an accomplice, pressing in from the left and right, occupying a group in front of Xi Bu. Lie Shizan broke through the crowd,挑動毛腿, and the enemy'

Complete Collection of Yuan Dynasty Zaju Dramas, Volume Three Published; "Collection of Poems from Eminent Women of the Ming Dynasty, Cui Lou Ji" to be Published Next Week 167

The transmission of Yuan Dynasty songs has been limited to only one type, "Selection of Yuan Songs". Over the past few centuries, those studying the songs have occasionally made discoveries. Mr. Dong Shoujing has compiled supplements, but the gains have been minimal. Lu Qian from Jiangning has spent ten years collecting Yuan and Ming Dynasty Zaju dramas and Sanqu poems, compiling them into two major collections. One of them is the "Complete Collection of Yuan Dynasty Zaju Dramas", consisting of eight volumes, with one volume published each month, included in the "Chinese Literature Rare Book Series". After the publication of the first volume, it was highly praised by readers. Mr. Wu Mei, a contemporary expert in the study of songs, even wrote an article recommending it, and its sales were very wide. Now, the third volume is being published, containing the works of Zheng Tingyu and Ma Zhiyuan, with more than 460 pages and nearly 400,000 words, printed in one thick volume. The retail price is only 60 cents for the popular edition and 80 cents for the special edition. Next week's publication will be the "Selection of Poems from Eminent Women of the Ming Dynasty, Cui Lou Ji", proofread by Shi Zhecun. It is also reported that the Shanghai Magazine Company, in response to requests from readers in various places, will continue to accept pre-orders for one month. Those who pay the pre-order price of seventeen yuan and a postal fee of one yuan and fifty cents can still be accommodated until the end of February.

Shanghai Biscuit, Candy, Canned Goods, and Bread Industry Association Holds Meeting 168

The Shanghai Biscuit, Candy, Canned Goods, and Bread Industry Association held a meeting of member representatives yesterday, attended by more than fifty companies. Le Fucheng was publicly elected as chairman. After the opening ceremony and reports on the work and purpose of the meeting, the following was discussed: The proposal to change to using the municipal standard of weight for unified pricing was resolved as follows: According to the old practice, calculations will still be based on pounds, converted with an addition of 11% per municipal catty, to be implemented uniformly from March 1st, in order to emphasize the seriousness of the regulations. The proposal to amend the articles of association based on the approval of the Ministry of Industry was resolved as follows: Members do not have the freedom to withdraw from the association. If businesses in the same industry resist joining the association, they must be ordered to fulfill the same obligations as members. Regarding the membership fees to be borne, a letter should be sent in advance to inform them, and then personnel should be sent to collect them. If they delay in paying, a petition should be filed with the court to issue a payment order according to law. If any member or non-member violates the resolutions, a petition must also be filed with the court to impose a fine for violation. Copies of the articles of association, both original and duplicate, should be filed with the Municipal Party Department and the Social Affairs Bureau for record and strict implementation. Due to the request of a majority of bread factories to join the association as members, the proposal to revise the name of the association was resolved as follows: This association has had a small number of bread factory members in the past. Now that a majority have joined, the words "bread" should be added to the name to reflect the actual situation, and the higher authorities should be notified for record. The meeting was adjourned after the discussions.

Record of the Meeting of the Fresh Pork Vendors Association 169

The Shanghai Fresh Pork Vendors Association held its 31st executive committee meeting the day before yesterday (the 8th). More than ten people attended, including Li Jinru, He Yusun, Tang Baoquan, and Chu Jiasheng. He Yusun was elected chairman. After the usual formalities, the chairman reported on the association's affairs. The following proposals were then discussed: Chairman Chen's letter stating that due to numerous affairs, he could not manage both his work and the association's affairs, and requested to resign from his positions as standing committee member and chairman, the proposal to approve the resignation. Resolved: The resignation is approved. The proposal to elect another committee member to fill the vacancies after Chairman Chen's resignation was resolved as follows: Committee member Liu Jingzhou was publicly elected to succeed as standing committee member and chairman. According to the notice from the Social Affairs Bureau, the association was scheduled to send responsible representatives to be questioned at 2:00 PM on the 10th of this month regarding the crackdown on live pig bristle pulling. The proposal to nominate someone to attend was resolved as follows: The association's executive director, Shi Yizheng, was nominated to attend as a representative. The meeting was adjourned.

Record of the First Executive Committee Meeting of the 38th Branch of the Municipal Federation 170

The 38th Branch of the Municipal Federation held its first executive committee meeting yesterday. More than ten people attended, including Zhang Wenkui, Ge Futian, and Chen Jingfeng. Luo Zheng chaired the meeting, and Fan Tianjin recorded the minutes. The chairman reported on the purpose of the meeting and the incoming documents. (A) Distribution of duties: Ge Futian, Luo Zheng, and Chen Qifen were appointed as representatives to the General Assembly; Zhang Wenkui, Chen Jingfeng, Jiang Ziyu, Chen Qifen, Zhang Xianfang, Liu Zhongying, and Wang Manyun were appointed as standing committee members; Luo Zheng, Chen Qifen, Zhang Wenkui, Chen Jingfeng, Jiang Ziyuan, and Zhang Ruzhou were appointed as general affairs committee members; Xu Zhixiang, Situ Jin, and Fei Jinfu were appointed as mediation committee members; Shen Yucheng, Chen Jisheng, and Fan Deyu were appointed as publicity committee members; and Zhu Yutao was appointed as secretary. (B) Discussion of proposals: The telephone company is implementing disguised price increases, and what should be done? Resolved: (A) Send a letter to the General Assembly for handling. (B) Notify members to solicit opinions and unanimously oppose the price increase. The economy is depressed, and member stores cannot maintain their operations, and have reported to the association, requesting assistance. Resolved: (A) Send a letter to the General Assembly to forward it to the Municipal Government, requesting the prompt promulgation of rent reduction orders. (B) Issue a statement. The proposal to solicit members was resolved as follows: Schedule a date for all committee members to go out to publicize and solicit members. The proposal to hire a voluntary legal counsel was resolved as follows: Hire Wang Manyun, [name unclear, possibly two or one name from characters] two big lawyers. The proposal to hire a voluntary medical advisor was resolved as follows: Hire Yang Yanhe and He Nengshi, two big doctors. The meeting was adjourned. The Hebei Native Place Association in Shanghai held its ninth general membership meeting at 2:00 PM yesterday to amend the association's articles of association and re-elect executive and supervisory committee members. More than a thousand people attended, including Wang Longzhang, a representative from the Municipal Party Department, and association members Qi Yunqing, Wang Fadong, and Li Shizeng (represented by Wang Bulun), as well as men, women, and children. Sun Bolan, Zhao Nangong, Jiang Zicheng, Dong Shouquan, and Wang Faqin were publicly elected as the presidium, with Zhen Ziguang as the master of ceremonies and Shen Yingshi and Wang Shouxian as recorders. After the usual formalities, Zhao Nangong first reported that a total of seventeen meetings were held in 1935, providing relief to fellow villagers and assisting 291 people in returning to their hometowns, 2,548 people were treated in hospitals, and 150 people graduated from literacy schools, as well as the financial situation. The Municipal Party Department representative Wang Longzhang delivered an instruction speech. The proposal to amend Article 14 of the articles of association, increasing the number of executive committee members to 37, with 11 alternates, and 11 supervisory committee members, with 3 alternates, was resolved and passed. The election ballots were cast, the ballot boxes were opened, and the votes were counted. Entertainment performances were also held. The meeting adjourned at 8:00 PM.
